   NM1.1a/ dharma.ekatānāḥ puruṣā yadāsan satyavādinaḥ /	NM1.1a/ Darma-.ekatAnAH puruzAH yat-A-Asan satya-vAdinaH /

   NMṃ3.1c/ niyuktena tu vaktavyam apakṣapatitaṃ vacaḥ // 1	NMM3.1c/ niyuktena tu vaktavyam apakza-patitam vacaH // 1
   NM3.2a/ yuktarūpaṃ bruvan sabhyo nāpnuyād dveṣakilbiṣe /	NM3.2a/ yukta-rUpam bruvan saByaH na-ApnuyAt dveza-kilbize /
   NM3.2c/ bruvāṇas tv anyathā sabhyas tad eva-ubhayam āpnuyāt // 2	NM3.2c/ bruvANaH tu anyaTA saByaH tat eva--uBayam ApnuyAt // 2
   NM3.3a/ rājā tu dhārmikān sabhyān niyuñjyāt suparīkṣitān /	NM3.3a/ rAjA tu DArmikAn saByAt niyuQjyAt su-parIkzitAn /

   NM3.4a/ dharmaśāstrārthakuśalāḥ kulīnāḥ satyavādinaḥ /	NM3.4a/ Darma-SAstra-arTa-kuSalAH kulInAH satya-vAdinaH /
   NM3.4c/ samāḥ śatrau ca mitre ca nṛpateḥ syuḥ sabhāsadaḥ // 4	NM3.4c/ samAH SatrO ca mitre ca nRpateH syuH saBAsadaH // 4
   NM3.5a/ tatpratiṣṭhaḥ smṛto dharmo dharmamūlaś ca pārthivaḥ /	NM3.5a/ tad-pratizWaH smRtaH DarmaH Darma-mUlaH ca pArTivaH /

   NM3.7a/ yatra dharmo hy adharmeṇa satyaṃ yatrānṛtena ca /	NM3.7a/ yatra DarmaH hi aDarmeNa satyam yatra-anRtena ca /

   NM3.9a/ sabhā vā na praveṣṭavyā vaktavyaṃ vā samañjasam /	NM3.9a/ saBA vA na pravezwavyAH vaktavyam vA samaQjasam /
   NM3.9c/ abruvan vibruvan vāpi naro bhavati kilbiṣī // 9	NM3.9c/ abruvan vibruvan vA-api naraH Bavati kilbizI // 9
   NM3.10a/ ye tu sabhyāḥ sabhāṃ gatvā tūṣṇīṃ dhyāyanta āsate /	NM3.10a/ ye tu saByAH saBAm gatvA tUzNIm DyAyantaH Asate /
   NM3.10c/ yathāprāptaṃ na bruvate sarve te 'anṛtavādinaḥ // 10	NM3.10c/ yaTAprAptam na bruvate sarve te aanRta-vAdinaH // 10
   NM3.11a/ pādo 'adharmasya kartāraṃ pādaḥ sākṣiṇam ṛcchati /	NM3.11a/ pAdaH aaDarmasya kartAram pAdaH sAkziNam RcCati /
   NM3.11c/ pādaḥ sabhāsadaḥ sarvān pādo rājānam ṛcchati // 11	NM3.11c/ pAdaH saBAsadaH sarvAn pAdaH rAjAnam RcCati // 11

   NM3.13c/ parokṣam arthavaikalyād bhāṣate yaḥ sabhāṃ gataḥ // 13	NM3.13c/ parokzam arTa-vEkalyAt BAzate yaH saBAm gataH // 13
   NM3.14a/ tasmāt sabhyaḥ sabhāṃ prāpya rāgadveṣavivarjitaḥ /	NM3.14a/ tasmAt saByaH saBAm prApya rAga-dveza-vivarjitaH /

   1. ṛṇādānam	1. RNa-AdAnam
   N1.01a/ ṛṇaṃ deyam adeyaṃ ca yena yatra yathā ca yat /	N1.01a/ RNam deyam adeyam ca yena yatra yaTA ca yat /
   N1.01c/ dānagrahaṇadharmāc ca ṛṇādānam iti smṛtam // 1	N1.01c/ dAna-grahaNa-DarmAt ca RNa-AdAnam iti smRtam // 1
   N1.02a/ pitary uparate putrā ṛṇaṃ dadyur yathāṃśataḥ /	N1.02a/ pitari uparate putrAH RNam dadyuH yaTA-aMSataH /

   N1.03a/ pitṛvyeṇāvibhaktena bhrātrā vā yad ṛṇaṃ kṛtam /	N1.03a/ pitRvyeNa-aviBaktena BrAtrA vA yat RNam kRtam /

   N1.04a/ kramād avyāhataṃ prāptaṃ putrair yan narṇam uddhṛtam /	N1.04a/ kramAt avyAhatam prAptam putrEH yat na-RNam udDRtam /

   N1.06a/ ataḥ putreṇa jātena svārtham utsṛjya yatnataḥ /	N1.06a/ atas putreNa jAtena sva-arTam utsRjya yatnatas /

   N1.08a/ na putrarṇaṃ pitā dadyād dadyāt putras tu paitṛkam /	N1.08a/ na putra-RNam pitA dadyAt dadyAt putraH tu pEtRkam /

   N1.11a/ nārvāg viṃśatimād varṣāt pitari proṣite sutaḥ /	N1.11a/ na-arvAk viMSatimAt varzAt pitari prozite sutaH /

   N1.12a/ dāpyaḥ pararṇam eko 'api jīvatsv adhikṛtaiḥ kṛtam /	N1.12a/ dApyaH para-RNam ekaH aapi jIvatsu aDikRtEH kRtam /

   N12.95c/ tyajan bhāryām avasthāpyo rājñā daṇḍena bhūyasā //	N12.95c/ tyajan BAryAm avasTApyaH rAjQA daNxena BUyasA //
   N12.96a/ ajñātadoṣeṇoḍhā yā nirgatā nānyam āśritā /	N12.96a/ ajQAta-dozeNa-UXA yA nirgatA na-anyam ASritAH /
   N12.96c/ bandhubhiḥ sā niyoktavyā nirbandhuḥ svayam āśrayet //	N12.96c/ banDuBiH sA niyoktavyA nirbanDuH svayam ASrayet //

   N12.98a/ aṣṭau varṣāṇy udīkṣeta brāhmaṇī proṣitaṃ patim /	N12.98a/ azwO varzANi udIkzeta brAhmaNI prozitam patim /

   N12.100a/ na śūdrāyāḥ smṛtaḥ kālo na ca dharmavyatikramaḥ /	N12.100a/ na SUdrAyAH smRtaH kAlaH na ca Darma-vyatikramaH /

   N12.101a/ apravṛttau smṛtaḥ dharma eṣa proṣitayoṣitām /	N12.101a/ apravRttO smRtaH DarmaH eza prozita-yozitAm /

   N12.102a/ prajāpravṛttau bhūtānāṃ sṛṣṭir eṣā prajāpateḥ /	N12.102a/ prajA-pravRttO BUtAnAm sRzwiH ezA prajApateH /
   N12.102c/ ato 'anyagamane strīṇām evaṃ doṣo na vidyate //	N12.102c/ atas aanya-gamane strINAm evam dozaH na vidyate //
   N12.103a/ ānulomyena varṇānāṃ yaj janma sa vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ /	N12.103a/ Anulomyena varNAnAm yat janma sa viDiH smRtaH /
   N12.103c/ prātilomyena yaj janma sa jñeyo varṇasaṃkaraḥ //	N12.103c/ prAtilomyena yat janma sa jQeyaH varNa-saMkaraH //
   N12.104a/ anantaraḥ smṛtaḥ putraḥ putra ekāntaras tathā /	N12.104a/ anantaraH smRtaH putraH putraH eka-antaraH taTA /
   N12.104c/ dvyantaraś cānulomyena tathaiva pratilomataḥ //	N12.104c/ dvi-antaraH ca-Anulomyena taTA-eva pratilomataH //

   N12.107a/ ambaṣṭho māgadhaś caiva kṣattā ca kṣatriyāsutāḥ /	N12.107a/ ambazWaH mAgaDaH ca-eva kzattA ca kzatriyA-sutAH /

   N12.109a/ sūtādyāḥ pratilomās tu ye jātipratilomajāḥ /	N12.109a/ sUta-AdyAH pratilomAH tu ye jAti-pratiloma-jAH /
   N12.109c/ te saṃkarāḥ śvapākādyās teṣāṃ triḥ saptako gaṇaḥ //	N12.109c/ te saMkarAH SvapAka-AdyAH tezAm tris saptakaH gaNaH //
   N12.110a/ savarṇo brāhmaṇīputraḥ kṣatriyāyām anantaraḥ /	N12.110a/ savarNaH brAhmaNI-putraH kzatriyAyAm anantaraH /
   N12.110c/ ambaṣṭhograu tathā putrāv evaṃ kṣatriyavaiśyayoḥ //	N12.110c/ ambazWa-ugrO taTA putrO evam kzatriya-vESyayoH //
   N12.111a/ ekāntaras tu dauṣṣanto vaiśyāyāṃ brāhmaṇāt sutaḥ /	N12.111a/ eka-antaraH tu dOzzantaH vESyAyAm brAhmaNAt sutaH /
   N12.111c/ śūdrāyāṃ kṣatriyāt tadvan niṣādo nāma jāyate //	N12.111c/ SUdrAyAm kzatriyAt tadvat nizAdaH nAma jAyate //
   N12.112a/ śūdrā pāraśavaṃ sūte brāhmaṇād uttaraṃ sutam /	N12.112a/ SUdrA pAraSavam sUte brAhmaNAt uttaram sutam /
   N12.112c/ ānulomyena varṇānāṃ putrā hy ete prakīrtitāḥ //	N12.112c/ Anulomyena varNAnAm putrAH hi ete prakIrtitAH //
   N12.113a/ sūtaś ca māgadhaś caiva putrāv āyogavas tathā /	N12.113a/ sUtaH ca mAgaDaH ca-eva putrO AyogavaH taTA /
   N12.113c/ prātilomyena varṇānāṃ tadvad ete 'apy anantarāḥ //	N12.113c/ prAtilomyena varNAnAm tadvat ete aapi anantarAH //
   N12.114a/ anantaraḥ smṛtaḥ sūto brāhmaṇyāṃ kṣatriyāt sutaḥ /	N12.114a/ anantaraH smRtaH sUtaH brAhmaNyAm kzatriyAt sutaH /
   N12.114c/ māgadhāyogavau tadvad dvī putrau vaiśyaśūdrayoḥ //	N12.114c/ mAgaDa-AyogavO tadvat dvI putrO vESya-SUdrayoH //
   N12.115a/ brāhmaṇy ekāntaraṃ vaiśyāt sūte vaidehakaṃ sutam /	N12.115a/ brAhmaNI eka-antaram vESyAt sUte vEdehakam sutam /
   N12.115c/ kṣattāraṃ kṣatriyā śūdrāt putram ekāntaraṃ tathā //	N12.115c/ kzattAram kzatriyA SUdrAt putram eka-antaram taTA //
   N12.116a/ dvyantaraḥ prātilomyena pāpiṣṭhaḥ sati saṃkare /	N12.116a/ dvi-antaraH prAtilomyena pApizWaH sati saMkare /
   N12.116c/ cāṇḍālo jāyate śūdrād brāhmaṇī yatra muhyati //	N12.116c/ cANxAlaH jAyate SUdrAt brAhmaNI yatra muhyati //
   N12.117a/ rājñā parīkṣyaṃ na yathā jāyate varṇasaṃkaraḥ /	N12.117a/ rAjQA parIkzyam na yaTA jAyate varNa-saMkaraH /
   N12.117c/ tasmād rājñā viśeṣeṇa trayī rakṣyā tu saṃkarāt //	N12.117c/ tasmAt rAjQA viSezeNa trayI rakzyA tu saMkarAt //
   13.dāyabhāgaḥ	13.dAya-BAgaH
   N13.1a/ vibhāgo 'arthasya pitryasya putrair yatra prakalpyate /	N13.1a/ viBAgaH aarTasya pitryasya putrEH yatra prakalpyate /
   N13.1c/ dāyabhāga iti proktaṃ tad vivādapadaṃ budhaiḥ //	N13.1c/ dAya-BAgaH iti proktam tat vivAda-padam buDEH //
   N13.2a/ pitary ūrdhvaṃ mṛte putrā vibhajeyur dhanaṃ pituḥ /	N13.2a/ pitari UrDvam mRte putrAH viBajeyuH Danam pituH /
   N13.2c/ mātur duhitaro 'abhāve duhitāṃ tadanvayaḥ //	N13.2c/ mAtuH duhitaraH aaBAve duhitAm tad-anvayaH //
   N13.3a/ mātur nivṛtte rajasi prattāsu bhaginīṣu ca /	N13.3a/ mAtuH nivRtte rajasi prattAsu BaginIzu ca /
   N13.3c/ niraṣṭe vāpy amaraṇe pitary uparataspṛhe //	N13.3c/ nirazwe vA-api amaraNe pitari uparata-spRhe //
   N13.4a/ pitaiva vā svayaṃ putrān vibhajed vayasi sthitaḥ /	N13.4a/ pitA-eva vA svayam putrAn viBajet vayasi sTitaH /
   N13.4c/ jyeṣṭhaṃ śreṣṭhavibhāgena yathā vāsya matir bhavet //	N13.4c/ jyezWam SrezWa-viBAgena yaTA vA-asya matiH Bavet //
   N13.5a/ bibhṛyād vecchataḥ sarvāñ jyeṣṭho bhrātā yathā pitā /	N13.5a/ biBRyAt vA-icCataH sarvAn jyezWaH BrAtA yaTA pitA /
   N13.5c/ bhrātā śaktaḥ kaniṣṭho vā śaktyapekṣaḥ kule kriyā //	N13.5c/ BrAtA SaktaH kanizWaH vA Sakti-apekzaH kule kriyA //
   N13.6a/ śauryabhāryādhane hitvā yac ca vidyādhanaṃ bhavet /	N13.6a/ SOrya-BAryA-Dane hitvA yat ca vidyA-Danam Bavet /
   N13.6c/ trīṇy etāny avibhājyāni prasādo yaś ca paitṛkaḥ //	N13.6c/ trINi etAni aviBAjyAni prasAdaH yaH ca pEtRkaH //
   N13.7a/ mātrā ca svadhanaṃ dattaṃ yasmai syāt prītipūrvakam /	N13.7a/ mAtrA ca sva-Danam dattam yasmE syAt prIti-pUrvakam /
   N13.7c/ tasyāpy eṣa vidhir dṛṣṭo mātāpīṣṭe yathā pitā //	N13.7c/ tasya-api eza viDiH dRzwaH mAtA-api-Izwe yaTA pitA //
   N13.8a/ adhyagnyadhyāvahanikaṃ bhartṛdāyas tathaiva ca /	N13.8a/ aDyagni-aDyAvahanikam BartR-dAyaH taTA-eva ca /
   N13.8c/ bhrātṛmātṛpitṛbhyaś ca ṣaḍvidhaṃ strīdhanaṃ smṛtam //	N13.8c/ BrAtR-mAtR-pitRByaH ca zaxviDam strIDanam smRtam //
   N13.9a/ strīdhanaṃ tadapatyānāṃ bhartṛgāmy aprajāsu ca /	N13.9a/ strIDanam tad-apatyAnAm BartR-gAmI aprajAsu ca /
   N13.9c/ brāhmādiṣu catuḥṣv āhuḥ pitṛgāmītareṣu tu //	N13.9c/ brAhma-Adizu catuHzu AhuH pitR-gAmi-itarezu tu //
   N13.10a/ kuṭumbaṃ bibhṛyād bhrātur yo vidyām adhigacchataḥ /	N13.10a/ kuwumbam biBRyAt BrAtuH yaH vidyAm aDigacCataH /
   N13.10c/ bhāgaṃ vidyādhanāt tasmāt sa labhetāśruto 'api san //	N13.10c/ BAgam vidyA-DanAt tasmAt sa laBeta-aSrutaH aapi san //
   N13.11a/ vaidyo 'avaidyāya nākāmo dadyād aṃśaṃ svato dhanāt /	N13.11a/ vEdyaH aavEdyAya na-akAmaH dadyAt aMSam svatas DanAt /
   N13.11c/ pitṛdravyaṃ tad āśritya na cet tena tad āhṛtam //	N13.11c/ pitR-dravyam tat ASritya na ced tena tat AhRtam //
   N13.12a/ dvāv āṃśau pratipadyeta vibhajann ātmanaḥ pitā /	N13.12a/ dvO AMSO pratipadyeta viBajan AtmanaH pitA /
   N13.12c/ samāṃśabhāginī mātā putrāṇāṃ syān mṛte patau //	N13.12c/ sama-aMSa-BAginI mAtA putrANAm syAt mRte patO //
   N13.13a/ jyeṣṭhāyāṃśo 'adhiko deyaḥ jyeṣṭhāya tu varaḥ smṛtaḥ /	N13.13a/ jyezWAya-aMSaH aaDikaH deyaH jyezWAya tu varaH smRtaH /
   N13.13c/ samāṃśabhājaḥ śeṣāḥ syur aprattā bhaginī tathā //	N13.13c/ sama-aMSa-BAjaH SezAH syuH aprattA BaginI taTA //
   N13.14a/ kṣetrajeṣv api putreṣu tadvaj jāteṣu dharmataḥ /	N13.14a/ kzetrajezu api putrezu tadvat jAtezu DarmataH /
   N13.14c/ varṇāvareṣv aṃśahānir ūḍhājāteṣv anukramāt //	N13.14c/ varNa-avarezu aMSa-hAniH UXa-ajAtezu anukramAt //
   N13.15a/ pitraiva tu vibhaktā ye hīnādhikasamair dhanaiḥ /	N13.15a/ pitrA-eva tu viBaktAH ye hIna-aDika-samEH DanEH /

   N13.16a/ kānīnaś ca sahoḍhaś ca gūḍhāyāṃ yaś ca jāyate /	N13.16a/ kAnInaH ca sahoXaH ca gUXAyAm yaH ca jAyate /
   N13.16c/ teṣāṃ voḍhāpitā jñeyas te ca bhāgaharāḥ smṛtāḥ //	N13.16c/ tezAm vA-UXA-pitA jQeyaH te ca BAga-harAH smRtAH //
   N13.17a/ ajñātapitṛko yaś ca kānīno 'anūḍhamātṛkaḥ /	N13.17a/ ajQAta-pitRkaH yaH ca kAnInaH aanUXa-mAtRkaH /
   N13.17c/ mātāmahāya dadyāt sa piṇḍaṃ rikthaṃ hareta ca //	N13.17c/ mAtAmahAya dadyAt sa piNxam rikTam hareta ca //
   N13.18a/ jātā ye tv aniyuktāyām ekena bahubhis tathā /	N13.18a/ jAtAH ye tu aniyuktAyAm ekena bahuBiH taTA /

   N13.19c/ aśulkopagatāyāṃ tu piṇḍadā voḍhur eva te //	N13.19c/ aSulka-upagatAyAm tu piNxa-dAH voXuH eva te //
   N13.20a/ pitṛdviṭ patitaḥ paṇḍo yaś ca syād aupapātikaḥ /	N13.20a/ pitR-dviz patitaH paNxaH yaH ca syAt OpapAtikaH /
   N13.20c/ aurasā api naite 'aṃśaṃ labheran kṣetrajāḥ kutaḥ //	N13.20c/ OrasAH api na-ete aaMSam laBeran kzetrajAH kutas //
   N13.21a/ dīrghatīvrāmayagrastā jaḍonmattāndhapaṅgavaḥ /	N13.21a/ dIrGa-tIvra-Amaya-grastAH jaxa-unmatta-anDa-paFgavaH /
   N13.21c/ bhartavyāḥ syuḥ kule caite tatputrās tv aṃśabhāginaḥ //	N13.21c/ BartavyAH syuH kule ca-ete tad-putrAH tu aMSa-BAginaH //
   N13.22a/ dvirāmuṣyāyaṇā dadyur dvābhyāṃ piṇḍodake pṛthak /	N13.22a/ dvis-AmuzyAyaNAH dadyuH dvAByAm piNxa-udake pRTak /
   N13.22c/ rikthād ardhāṃśam ādadyur bījikṣetrikayos tathā //	N13.22c/ rikTAt arDa-aMSam AdadyuH bIji-kzetrikayoH taTA //
   N13.23a/ saṃsṛṣṭināṃ tu yo bhāgas teṣām eva sa iṣyate /	N13.23a/ saMsRzwinAm tu yaH BAgaH tezAm eva saH izyate /
   N13.23c/ ato 'anyathāṃśabhājo hi nirbījiṣv itarān iyāt //	N13.23c/ atas aanyaTA-aMSa-BAjaH hi nirbIjizu itarAn iyAt //
   N13.24a/ bhrātām aprajaḥ preyāt kaścic cet pravrajet tu vā /	N13.24a/ BrAtAm aprajaH preyAt kaScid ced pravrajet tu vA /

   N13.25a/ bharaṇam cāsya kurvīran strīṇām ā jīvitakṣayāt /	N13.25a/ BaraNam ca-asya kurvIran strINAm A jIvita-kzayAt /
   N13.25c/ rakṣanti śayyāṃ bhartuś ced ācchindyur itarāsu tu //	N13.25c/ rakzanti SayyAm BartuH ced AcCindyuH itarAsu tu //
   N13.26a/ syād yasya duhitā tasyāḥ pitraṃśo bharaṇe mataḥ /	N13.26a/ syAt yasya duhitA tasyAH pitR-aMSaH BaraNe mataH /
   N13.26c/ ā saṃskārād bhajed enāṃ parato bibhṛyāt patiḥ //	N13.26c/ A saMskArAt Bajet enAm paratas biBRyAt patiH //
   N13.27a/ mṛte bhartary aputrāyāḥ patipakṣaḥ prabhuḥ striyāḥ /	N13.27a/ mRte Bartari aputrAyAH pati-pakzaH praBuH striyAH /
   N13.27c/ viniyogātmarakṣāsu bharaṇe ca sa īśvaraḥ //	N13.27c/ viniyoga-Atma-rakzAsu BaraNe ca saH ISvaraH //
   N13.28a/ parikṣīṇe patikule nirmaṇuṣye nirāśraye /	N13.28a/ parikzINe pati-kule nirmaNuzye nirASraye /
   N13.28c/ tatsapiṇḍeṣu vāsatsu pitṛpakṣaḥ prabhuḥ striyāḥ //	N13.28c/ tad-sapiNxezu vA-asatsu pitR-pakzaH praBuH striyAH //
   N13.29a/ pakṣadvayāvasāne tu rājā bhartā smṛtaḥ striyāḥ /	N13.29a/ pakza-dvaya-avasAne tu rAjA BartA smRtaH striyAH /
   N13.29c/ sa tasyā bharaṇaṃ kuryān nigṛhṇīyāt pathaś cyutām //	N13.29c/ sa tasyAH BaraNam kuryAt nigRhNIyAt paTaH cyutAm //
   N13.30a/ svātantryād vipraṇaśyanti kule jātā api striyaḥ /	N13.30a/ svAtantryAt vipraNaSyanti kule jAtAH api striyaH /
   N13.30c/ asvātantryam atas tāsāṃ prajāpatir akalpayat //	N13.30c/ asvAtantryam atas tAsAm prajApatiH akalpayat //
   N13.31a/ pitā rakṣati kaumāre bhartā rakṣati yauvane /	N13.31a/ pitA rakzati kOmAre BartA rakzati yOvane /
   N13.31c/ putrā rakṣanti vaidhavye na strī svātantryam arhati //	N13.31c/ putrAH rakzanti vEDavye na strI svAtantryam arhati //
   N13.32a/ yac chiṣṭaṃ pitṛdāyebhyo dattva rṇaṃ paitṛkaṃ ca yat /	N13.32a/ yat Sizwam pitR-dAyeByaH dattva rNam pEtRkam ca yat /
   N13.32c/ bhrātṛbhis tad vibhaktavyam ṛṇī na syād yathā pitā //	N13.32c/ BrAtRBiH tat viBaktavyam RNI na syAt yaTA pitA //
   N13.33a/ yeṣāṃ ca na kṛtāḥ pitrā saṃskāravidhayaḥ kramāt /	N13.33a/ yezAm ca na kRtAH pitrA saMskAra-viDayaH kramAt /
   N13.33c/ kartavyā bhrātṛbhis teṣāṃ paitṛkād eva te dhanāt //	N13.33c/ kartavyA BrAtRBiH tezAm pEtRkAt eva te DanAt //
   N13.34a/ avidyamāne pitrye 'arthe svāṃśād uddhṛtya vā punaḥ /	N13.34a/ avidyamAne pitrye aarTe sva-aMSAt udDRtya vA punar /
   N13.34c/ avaśyakāryāḥ saṃskārā bhrātāṃ pūrvasaṃskṛtaiḥ //	N13.34c/ avaSya-kAryAH saMskArAH BrAtAm pUrva-saMskRtEH //

   N20.31c/ tasmāt satyena bhagavañ jaleśa trātum arhasi // 31	N20.31c/ tasmAt satyena Bagavan jaleSa trAtum arhasi // 31
   [viṣam]	[vizam]
   N20.32a/ ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi viṣasya vidhim uttamam /	N20.32a/ atas param pravakzyAmi vizasya viDim uttamam /
   N20.32c/ tulayitvā viṣaṃ pūrvaṃ deyam etad dhimāgame // 32	N20.32c/ tulayitvA vizam pUrvam deyam etat DimAgame // 32
   N20.33a/ na pūrvāhṇe na madhyāhne na saṃdhyāyāṃ tu dharmavit /	N20.33a/ na pUrvAhNe na maDyAhne na saMDyAyAm tu Darma-vid /
   N20.33c/ śaradgrīṣmavasanteṣu varṣāsu ca na dāpayet // 33	N20.33c/ Sarad-grIzma-vasantezu varzAsu ca na dApayet // 33
   N20.34a/ bhagnaṃ ca dāritaṃ caiva dhūpitaṃ miśritaṃ tathā /	N20.34a/ Bagnam ca dAritam ca-eva DUpitam miSritam taTA /
   N20.34c/ kālakūṭam alaṃbuṃ ca viṣaṃ yatnena varjayet // 34	N20.34c/ kAlakUwam alaMbum ca vizam yatnena varjayet // 34
   N20.35a/ śārṅgahaimavataṃ śastaṃ gandhavarṇarasānvitam /	N20.35a/ SArFga-hEmavatam Sastam ganDa-varNa-rasa-anvitam /
   N20.35c/ mahādoṣavate deyaṃ rājñā tattvabubhutsayā // 35	N20.35c/ mahA-dozavate deyam rAjQA tattva-buButsayA // 35
   N20.36a/ na bālāturavṛddheṣu naiva svalpāparādhiṣu /	N20.36a/ na bAla-Atura-vRdDezu na-eva su-alpa-aparADizu /
   N20.36c/ viṣasya tu yavān sapta dadyāc chodye ghṛtaplutān // 36	N20.36c/ vizasya tu yavAn sapta dadyAt Codye GRta-plutAn // 36
   N20.37a/ viṣasya palaṣaḍbhāgād bhāgo viṃśatimas tu yaḥ /	N20.37a/ vizasya pala-zaz-BAgAt BAgaH viMSatimaH tu yaH /
   N20.37c/ tam aṣṭabhāgahīnaṃ tu śodhye dadyād ghṛtaplutam // 37	N20.37c/ tam azwa-BAga-hInam tu SoDye dadyAt GRta-plutam // 37
   N20.38a/ yathoktena vidhānena viprān sprṣṭvānumoditaḥ /	N20.38a/ yaTA-uktena viDAnena viprAn sprzwvA-anumoditaH /
   N20.38c/ sopavāsaś ca khādeta devabrāhmaṇasaṃnidhau // 38	N20.38c/ sa-upavAsaH ca KAdeta deva-brAhmaNa-saMniDO // 38
   N20.39a/ viṣaṃ vegaklamāpetaṃ sukhena yadi jīryate /	N20.39a/ vizam vega-klama-apetam suKena yadi jIryate /
   N20.39c/ viśuddham iti taṃ jñātvā rājā satkṛtya mokṣayet // 39	N20.39c/ viSudDam iti tam jQAtvA rAjA satkRtya mokzayet // 39
   N20.40a/ tvaṃ viṣa brahmaṇaḥ putraḥ satyadharmaratau sthitaḥ /	N20.40a/ tvam viza brahmaNaH putraH satya-Darma-ratO sTitaH /
   N20.40c/ śodhayainaṃ naraṃ pāpāt satyenāsyāmṛtībhava // 40	N20.40c/ SoDaya-enam naram pApAt satyena-asya-amRtIBavaH // 40
   [kośaḥ]	[koSaH]
   N20.41a/ ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi kośasya vidhim uttamam // 41	N20.41a/ atas param pravakzyAmi koSasya viDim uttamam // 41
   N20.42a/ pūrvāhṇe sopavāsasya snātasyārdrapaṭasya ca /	N20.42a/ pUrvAhNe sa-upavAsasya snAtasya-Ardra-pawasya ca /
   N20.42c/ saśūkasyāvyasaninaḥ kośapānaṃ vidhīyate // 42	N20.42c/ sa-SUkasya-avyasaninaH koSa-pAnam viDIyate // 42
   N20.43a/ yadbhaktaḥ so 'abhiyuktaḥ syāt taddaivatyaṃ tu pāyayet /	N20.43a/ yad-BaktaH saH aaBiyuktaH syAt tad-dEvatyam tu pAyayet /
   N20.43c/ saptāhād yasya dṛśyate dvisaptāhena vā punaḥ /	N20.43c/ sapta-ahAt yasya dRSyate dvi-sapta-ahena vA punar /
   N20.43e/ pratyātmikaṃ tu yatkiṃcit saiva tasya vibhāvanā // 43	N20.43e/ pratyAtmikam tu yat-kiMcid sA-eva tasya viBAvanA // 43
   N20.44a/ dvisaptāhāt paraṃ yasya mahad vā vaikṛtaṃ bhavet /	N20.44a/ dvi-sapta-ahAt param yasya mahat vA vEkRtam Bavet /
   N20.44c/ nābhiyojyaḥ sa viduṣāṃ kṛtakālavyatikramāt // 44	N20.44c/ na-aBiyojyaH sa viduzAm kRta-kAla-vyatikramAt // 44
   N20.45a/ mahāparādhe nirdharme kṛtaghne klībakutsite /	N20.45a/ mahA-aparADe nirDarme kRtaGne klIba-kutsite /
   N20.45c/ nāstikavrātyadāseṣu kośapānaṃ vivarjayet // 45	N20.45c/ nAstika-vrAtya-dAsezu koSa-pAnam vivarjayet // 45
   N20.46a/ yathoktena prakāreṇa pañca divyāni dharmavit /	N20.46a/ yaTA-uktena prakAreNa paQca divyAni Darma-vid /
   N20.46c/ dadyād rājābhiyuktānāṃ pretya ceha ca nandati // 46	N20.46c/ dadyAt rAja-aBiyuktAnAm pretya ca-iha ca nandati // 46
   N20.47a/ na viṣaṃ brāhmaṇe dadyān na lohaṃ kṣatriyo haret /	N20.47a/ na vizam brAhmaNe dadyAt na loham kzatriyaH haret /
   N20.47c/ na nimajjyāpsu vaiśyaś ca śūdraḥ kośaṃ na pāyayet // 47	N20.47c/ na nimajjya-apsu vESyaH ca SUdraH koSam na pAyayet // 47
   N20.48a/ varṣāsu na viṣaṃ dadyāt hemante nāpsu majjayet /	N20.48a/ varzAsu na vizam dadyAt hemante na-apsu majjayet /
   N20.48c/ na lohaṃ hārayed grīṣme na kośaṃ pāyayen niśi //	N20.48c/ na loham hArayet grIzme na koSam pAyayet niSi //
   48nāradīyadharmaśāstraḥ samāptaḥ.	48nAradIya-Darma-SAstraH samAptaH.
